Sam Rockwell, a versatile actor whose career has spanned decades, has graced our screens in a host of unforgettable roles. From quirky, comedic characters to serious, dramatic portrayals, Rockwell has proven his ability to captivate audiences time and time again. Join us as we revisit some of the most notable movies in Sam Rockwell's filmography and delve into the intricacies that make each one worth watching.

## 1. [Clownhouse (1989)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/clownhouse-1989?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=clownhouse-1989&utm_term=clownhouse-1989)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/clownhouse-1989?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=clownhouse-1989&amp;utm_term=clownhouse-1989"><img alt="clownhouse-tt0094886-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/clownhouse-tt0094886-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Clownhouse" takes a chilling turn just before Halloween as three young brothers are left alone amidst the festivities of the season. Unbeknownst to them, a sinister plan unfolds as three menacing individuals, recently escaped from a mental institution and wearing the stolen guises of some murdered circus clowns, set their sights on terrorizing the isolated family. As reality blurs with their worst nightmares, this family soon finds themselves in a race against time to confront and overcome their new and deadly adversaries. With a runtime of 1h 21min, "Clownhouse" features an ensemble cast, led by promising actors Nathan Forrest Winters, Brian McHugh, and Sam Rockwell. Written and directed by Victor Salva, this psychological horror film delves into the themes of innocence, sanity, and the terror of a home invasion. As an R-rated film, "Clownhouse" has garnered critical acclaim, earning two nominations. Don't miss this spine-tingling tale, where the clowns are anything but harmless and where the stakes are as high as life or death. 



<br>

- Genres: Horror
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 21min
- Directed by: Victor Salva
- Starring: Nathan Forrest Winters, Brian McHugh, Sam Rockwell
- Box Office:
 - Budget: $200,000 (estimated)

## 2. [Last Exit to Brooklyn (1989)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/last-exit-to-brooklyn-1989?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=last-exit-to-brooklyn-1989&utm_term=last-exit-to-brooklyn-1989)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/last-exit-to-brooklyn-1989?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=last-exit-to-brooklyn-1989&amp;utm_term=last-exit-to-brooklyn-1989"><img alt="last-exit-to-brooklyn-tt0097714-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/last-exit-to-brooklyn-tt0097714-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Last Exit to Brooklyn" is a gripping drama set in the volatile streets of 1950s New York City. Amidst union corruption and violence, the protagonist, a troubled prostitute, falls in love with a mysterious client. Intriguingly, the story intertwines with another character's journey of discovering his own sexuality. This emotionally charged depiction of a turbulent time offers an unflinching portrayal of urban life and human vulnerability. Uli Edel's direction and Hubert Selby Jr. 's writing combine to create a striking cinematic experience, bolstered by the powerful performances of its ensemble cast, including Jennifer Jason Leigh, Stephen Lang, and Burt Young. Embodying raw grit and social commentary, "Last Exit to Brooklyn" was rightly honored with several prestigious awards. 



<br>

- Genres: Drama
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 42min
- Directed by: Uli Edel
- Starring: Jennifer Jason Leigh, Stephen Lang, Burt Young

## 3. [Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles (1990)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-1990?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-1990&utm_term=teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-1990)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-1990?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-1990&amp;utm_term=teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-1990"><img alt="teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-tt0100758-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-tt0100758-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles" is a thrilling action-adventure-comedy film that explores the extraordinary adventures of four mutant turtles: Leonardo, Raphael, Donatello, and Michelangelo. The film, directed by Steve Barron and based on the characters created by Kevin Eastman and Peter Laird, brings the beloved 90s animated series to life. Released in 1990, the movie has become a cult classic, offering its audience an unforgettable experience filled with humor, excitement, and heart. The story follows the turtles as they emerge from the shadows, working together with a skilled rat named Splinter to protect New York City from a gang of criminal ninjas. The film stars a talented ensemble cast, including Judith Hoag as April O'Neil, Elias Koteas as Casey Jones, and Josh Pais as Raphael. With a runtime of 1h 33min and a content rating of PG, the movie delivers an exciting, family-friendly experience. The film has received a 6.8 IMDb rating out of 103,342 votes, boasting an impressive box office performance that has earned it a place in pop culture history. Since its release, "Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles" has inspired numerous sequels and adaptations, making it a beloved series and a must-watch for fans of all ages. In summary, "Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles" is a timeless, fun-filled adventure that offers a unique blend of action, comedy, and excitement. The film delivers a powerful message about teamwork and loyalty, making it a perfect choice for audiences seeking a thrilling, enjoyable experience. 



<br>

- Genres: Action, Adventure, Comedy
- Rated: PG
- Runtime: 1h 33min

## 4. [Strictly Business (1991)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/strictly-business-1991?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=strictly-business-1991&utm_term=strictly-business-1991)

<br>

Strictly Business (1991) is a comedic exploration of the ups and downs of friendship and the pursuit of love. The film follows the journey of an ambitious Black businessman and his street-smart friend, whose unconventional bond takes an unexpected turn when a stunningly attractive waitress catches the professional's eye. With a runtime of 1 hour 23 minutes and a PG-13 rating, this engaging romantic comedy is sure to leave you entertained and enthralled. Featuring a talented ensemble cast including Tommy Davidson, Joseph C. Phillips, and Anne-Marie Johnson, Strictly Business is a delightful escape into the world of romance and ambition.

## 5. [Happy Hell Night (1991)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/happy-hell-night-1991?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=happy-hell-night-1991&utm_term=happy-hell-night-1991)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/happy-hell-night-1991?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=happy-hell-night-1991&amp;utm_term=happy-hell-night-1991"><img alt="happy-hell-night-tt0236283-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/happy-hell-night-tt0236283-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Happy Hell Night" is a thrilling horror flick that unleashes its terror in the guise of a fraternity-hazing prank gone awry. Set against the backdrop of Winfield College's Halloween party, a psychotic killer now reigns supreme, meting out blood-soaked vengeance on the coeds. What starts as a harmless evening of revelry quickly escalates into a relentless nightmare, as the body count rises and fear grips every heart. This suspenseful, action-packed movie, replete with bare-chested men, is directed by Brian Owens and penned by Michael Fitzpatrick, Brian Owens, and Ron Petersen. The film stars Larry Robinson, Lisa Nichols, and a young Sam Rockwell, with production taking place across Canada and Yugoslavia. With a runtime of 1 hours and 27 minutes, "Happy Hell Night" promises to keep you on the edge of your seat as you immerse yourself in the chilling world of a killer on the loose. If you're a fan of suspenseful mysteries, or simply looking for a thrilling escape, this film is sure to satisfy your craving for fear. 



<br>

## 6. [In the Soup (1992)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/in-the-soup-1992?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=in-the-soup-1992&utm_term=in-the-soup-1992)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/in-the-soup-1992?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=in-the-soup-1992&amp;utm_term=in-the-soup-1992"><img alt="in-the-soup-tt0104503-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/in-the-soup-tt0104503-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"In the Soup" (1992) tells the story of struggling filmmaker Adolpho Rollo, a New Yorker with a vivid imagination and a head full of cinematic dreams. When he's not envisioning groundbreaking works of art, he struggles to pay rent for the dingy New York apartment he calls home. A chance encounter with a mysterious and enigmatic film producer offers him an opportunity to bring one of his ideas to the big screen. Along the way, he falls for a beautiful female cashier and forms strange, unexpected alliances. This offbeat comedy-drama, directed by Alexandre Rockwell and starring Steve Buscemi, Seymour Cassel, and Jennifer Beals, offers a witty, engaging look at the trials and tribulations of the independent film world. With a runtime of 1h 36min and an R content rating, "In the Soup" boasts an appealing blend of wit, drama, and humor that keeps viewers entertained from start to finish. It was well-received at the box office, earning $256,249 globally despite having no reported budget. The film also received critical acclaim, earning 5 wins and 3 nominations at various awards ceremonies. For fans of similar movies like "Trees Lounge, " "Living in Oblivion, " and "Stranger Than Paradise, " "In the Soup" is a must-watch gem worth discovering. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Drama
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 36min
- Directed by: Alexandre Rockwell
- Starring: Steve Buscemi, Seymour Cassel, Jennifer Beals

## 7. [Jack and His Friends (1992)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/jack-and-his-friends-1992?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=jack-and-his-friends-1992&utm_term=jack-and-his-friends-1992)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/jack-and-his-friends-1992?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=jack-and-his-friends-1992&amp;utm_term=jack-and-his-friends-1992"><img alt="jack-and-his-friends-tt0104538-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/jack-and-his-friends-tt0104538-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

Jack and His Friends (1992) is a unique, offbeat comedy that delves into the lives of a diverse group of characters during a most unusual weekend. Directed by Bruce Ornstein, this R-rated film stars Paul Barry, Alison Fraser, and Allen Garfield in a story that unfolds when Jack, a middle-aged, overweight shoe store owner, encounters Rosie and Louie, two small-time criminals on the run. Forced to kidnap Jack, the trio use his off-season, deserted vacation house as a temporary hideout. As the story progresses, an unlikely camaraderie forms between these individuals, leading to a whirlwind of events full of surprises and unexpected turns. With its blend of humor, suspense, and unconventional storytelling, Jack and His Friends (1992) offers an engaging and entertaining viewing experience. The film boasts notable performances by the lead actors and a witty script by Ornstein and Elle Kamihira. As the characters forge bonds in the face of adversity, this thought-provoking comedy is sure to leave a lasting impression on viewers. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 33min
- Directed by: Bruce Ornstein

- Box Office:
 - Budget: $1,000,000 (estimated)

## 8. [Light Sleeper (1992)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/light-sleeper-1992?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=light-sleeper-1992&utm_term=light-sleeper-1992)

<br>

"Light Sleeper" is a gripping crime drama released in 1992. The film, directed and written by the renowned Paul Schrader, delves into the life of a drug dealer who, after encountering various life-changing situations, begins to question his profession. Set amidst a backdrop of Miami's seedy underbelly, the movie is a compelling exploration of crime, morality, and the human condition. Willem Dafoe stars as the conflicted protagonist, supported by a brilliant performance from Susan Sarandon as his old flame. The film, which also boasts performances from Dana Delany, navigates themes of love, loyalty, and redemption in a world where survival is everything. Despite its intense, crime-ridden aesthetic, "Light Sleeper" subtly probes deeper issues of life, choice, and fate. Its engaging plot and powerful performances make it a must-watch for fans of the crime genre. 



<br>

## 9. [The Search for One-eye Jimmy (1994)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-1994?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-1994&utm_term=the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-1994)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-1994?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-1994&amp;utm_term=the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-1994"><img alt="the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-tt0117577-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-search-for-one-eye-jimmy-tt0117577-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"The Search for One-eye Jimmy" is a 1994 comedy revolving around a student filmmaker, Les, who decides to create a documentary about his old neighborhood in Brooklyn. The story takes an interesting turn when a local Vietnam War veteran, One-eye Jimmy, goes missing. Les switches gears and starts making a film about Jimmy and the people involved in the search for him. This engaging narrative showcases the creative process of a documentary filmmaker and delves into the lives of the characters in this close-knit community. Featuring notable stars like Holt McCallany, Michael Badalucco, and Nicholas Turturro, "The Search for One-eye Jimmy" is a directorial debut by Sam Henry Kass that offers an in-depth look into the heart of New York City. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 24min
- Directed by: Sam Henry Kass
- Starring: Holt McCallany, Michael Badalucco, Nicholas Turturro
- Box Office:
 - Gross USA: $71,314
 - Opening Weekend USA: $19,432
 - Cumulative Worldwide Gross: $71,314
- IMDb Rating: 6.0

The characters, brought to life by an impressive ensemble cast, navigate the complexities and nuances of human emotions and interactions, while exploring themes of love, compassion, violence, and loss. Each vignette offers a unique and unforgettable snapshot of life in the Big Apple, resulting in a compelling and thought-provoking cinematic experience. With direction by the talented Bob Balaban, Patricia Benoit, and Julie Dash, and a screenplay by Adam Brooks, John Guare, and Lynn Grossman, SUBWAYStories: Tales from the Underground is a must-watch for those who appreciate character-driven storytelling and powerful performances. The film stars the likes of Bill Irwin, KRS-One, and Tina North, and is presented by Clinica Estetico, HBO NYC Productions, and Ten in a Car Productions. Originally released on August 17, 1997, SUBWAYStories: Tales from the Underground earned an IMDb rating of 6.5 and garnered critical acclaim, receiving multiple awards for its captivating narrative and compelling depiction of life underground. If you're a fan of anthology dramas or simply love captivating stories that take place in the iconic New York City subway, SUBWAYStories: Tales from the Underground is an unmissable cinematic gem that transports its audience into the heart of the city that never sleeps.

Makuhari Media, responsible for producing the documentary, demonstrates their commitment to shedding light on the complexities and injustices surrounding university athletics in the United States. "Schooled: The Price of College Sports" is an intriguing exploration of this compelling topic, posing critical questions about fairness, valuation, and the underlying role college sports plays in the broader culture. With a sterling IMDb rating of 7.8, it's evident that this insightful documentary has struck a chord with audiences. The film, directed by Taika Waititi and awarded an Oscar, tells the story of a young German boy named Jojo (Roman Griffin Davis) who discovers that his mother (Scarlett Johansson) is hiding a Jewish girl (Thomasin McKenzie) in their home. As a member of the Hitler Youth, Jojo is shocked and conflicted by this revelation, which forces him to confront his beliefs and the beliefs of his imaginary friend, Adolf Hitler. With elements of satire and dark humor, "Jojo Rabbit" delves into themes of friendship, family, and the power of love in the most trying of circumstances. The film's exceptional cast, including Scarlett Johansson's Oscar-nominated performance, breathes life into its nuanced portrayal of love, loss, and identity in a world divided by hate and prejudice. With a runtime of 108 minutes, "Jojo Rabbit" is a stunning and impactful examination of humanity and our capacity for empathy and understanding in times of darkness. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Drama, War
- Rated: PG-13
- Runtime: 1h 48min
- Directed by: Taika Waititi
